ADAPTATION OF LAWS ORDERS PART IhP PREFACE This volume reproduces the text of various Orders (as amended from time to time) issued-under the Constitution of India up to the 2002. This edition consists of Part I and Part II. Part I reproduces the text of Constitutional Orders other than the Adaptation of Laws Orders. Part I1 consists of the Adaptation of Laws Orders issued under the Constitution and the Acts relating to territorial adjustments and formations of new States. SUBHASH C.
